<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Foreigners_2016.E2.80.9317">Foreigners 2016–17</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Maccabi_Tel_Aviv_F.C.&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Foreigners 2016–17">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Only up to Six non-Israeli nationals can be in an Israeli club squad (only five can play at the same time). Those with Jewish ancestry (e.g., <a href="/wiki/Egor_Filipenko" title="Egor Filipenko">Egor Filipenko</a>), married to an Israeli or have played in Israel for an extended period of time, can claim a passport or permanent residency which would allow them to play with Israeli status.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (December 2015)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup></p>
<ul>
<li><span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/Argentina" title="Argentina"><img alt="Argentina" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="500" data-file-width="800" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1a/Flag_of_Argentina.svg/23px-Flag_of_Argentina.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1a/Flag_of_Argentina.svg/35px-Flag_of_Argentina.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1a/Flag_of_Argentina.svg/46px-Flag_of_Argentina.svg.png 2x" width="23"/></a></span> <a href="/wiki/Ezequiel_%C3%93scar_Scarione" title="Ezequiel Óscar Scarione">Óscar Scarione</a></li>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Records">Records</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Maccabi_Tel_Aviv_F.C.&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Records">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul>
<li><b>Seasons in top division</b> – 65 (1949–present), (only team that has never been relegated)</li>
<li><b>Lowest league position</b> – 12 (1987–88)</li>
<li><b>Double seasons</b> – 7 (1946–47, 1953–54, 1957–58, 1969–1970, 1976–77, 1995–96, 2014–15)</li>
<li><b>Runner-up seasons</b> – 10 (1954–55, 1959–60, 1965–66, 1968–1969, 1973–74, 1992–93, 1993–94, 1998–99, 2003–04, 2015–16)</li>
<li><b>State Cup final appearances</b> – 35 (including victories)</li>
<li><b>Toto Cup final appearances</b> – 7 (including victories)</li>
<li><b>Invincible seasons</b> – 2 (1953–54, 1957–58), (no losses in the league and the State Cup)</li>
<li><b>Biggest 'undefeated' streak in the league</b> – 44 matches (11/10/51 – 03/05/55)</li>
<li><b>Biggest 'undefeated away matches' streak in the league</b> – 34 (07/16/49 – 03/05/55)</li>
<li><b>Win record for season</b> – 30 (1966–68)</li>
<li><b>Loss record for season</b> – 14 (2007–08, 2011–12)</li>
<li><b>Most points in a season</b> – 88 (1993–94)</li>
<li><b>Most 'league goals for' in a season (club)</b> – 103 (1949–50)</li>
<li><b>Most 'league goals against' in a season (club)</b> – 53 (1990–91)</li>
<li><b>Lowest number of 'league goals against' in a season (club)</b> – 11 (1953–54)</li>
<li><b>Most league goals differential in a season (club)</b> – 85 (1949–50), (103–18)</li>
<li><b>All time League goals</b> – 3114 (since 1948)</li>
<li><b>Biggest 'no goals against' streak in league matches</b> – 730 minutes (2014–15)</li>
<li><b>Biggest 'league matches won' streak since season start</b> – 11 (1993–94)</li>
<li><b>Highest point lead above runner-up in the end of the season</b> – 16 (2013–14)</li>
<li><b>Most goals in a season (player)</b> – 35, <a href="/wiki/Eran_Zahavi" title="Eran Zahavi">Eran Zahavi</a>, 2015–16</li>
<li><b>Biggest win</b> – 13–0 vs <a href="/wiki/Maccabi_Rishon_LeZion_F.C." title="Maccabi Rishon LeZion F.C.">Maccabi Rishon LeZion</a>, 1950</li>
<li><b>Biggest defeat</b> – 10–0 vs <a href="/wiki/Maccabi_Haifa_F.C." title="Maccabi Haifa F.C.">Maccabi Haifa</a>, 1988</li>
<li><b>Biggest home win</b> – 13–0 vs <a href="/wiki/Maccabi_Rishon_LeZion_F.C." title="Maccabi Rishon LeZion F.C.">Maccabi Rishon LeZion</a>, 1950</li>
<li><b>Biggest home defeat</b> – 4–0 vs <a href="/wiki/Hapoel_Acre_F.C." title="Hapoel Acre F.C.">Hapoel Acre</a>, 2006</li>
<li><b>Biggest away win</b> – 7–0 vs <a href="/wiki/Hapoel_Haifa_F.C." title="Hapoel Haifa F.C.">Hapoel Haifa</a>, 1994</li>
<li><b>Biggest away defeat</b> – 10–0 vs <a href="/wiki/Maccabi_Haifa_F.C." title="Maccabi Haifa F.C.">Maccabi Haifa</a>, 1988</li>
<li><b>Biggest win in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/European_football" title="European football">UEFA Competitions</a></b> – 6–0 vs <a href="/wiki/FK_%C5%BDalgiris" title="FK Žalgiris">FK Žalgiris</a> (2001) and <a href="/wiki/FK_%C5%BDeljezni%C4%8Dar_Sarajevo" title="FK Željezničar Sarajevo">Željezničar</a> (2011)</li>
<li><b>Biggest defeat in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/European_football" title="European football">UEFA Competitions</a></b> – 5–1 vs <a href="/wiki/FC_Bayern_Munich" title="FC Bayern Munich">Bayern Munich</a> (2004) and <a href="/wiki/Be%C5%9Fikta%C5%9F_J.K." title="Beşiktaş J.K.">Beşiktaş</a> (2011)</li>
<li><b>All-time top scorer</b> – <a href="/wiki/Avi_Nimni" title="Avi Nimni">Avi Nimni</a>, 174</li>
<li><b>All-time most appearances</b> – <a href="/wiki/Menachem_Bello" title="Menachem Bello">Menachem Bello</a>, 498</li>
</ul>
